GSR Usage
---------

GSR Component:
   The local reset signal 'core_rst_n' of the design has been inferred as Global
        Set Reset (GSR). The reset signal used for GSR control is 'core_rst_n'.

GSR Property:
   The design components with GSR property set to ENABLED will respond to global
        set reset while the components with GSR property set to DISABLED will
        not.

Components not on inferred reset domain but have GSR property enabled
---------------------------------------------------------------------

These components have the GSR property set to ENABLED and are not on the
     inferred reset domain. The components will respond to the unrelated reset
     signal 'core_rst_n' via the GSR component.

Type and number of components of the type:
   Register = 7

Type and instance name of component:
   Register : pcie/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_trnc/u1_rxintf/rx_data_1_CF1_1

   Register : pcie/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_trnc/u1_rxintf/rx_data_1_CF1_0
   Register : pcie/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dll/u1_rxtp/phy_l0_rp

   Register : pcie/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dll/u1_txtdp/u1_td_mux/tdata7_CF2_1
   Register : pcie/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dll/u1_txtdp/u1_td_mux/tdata7_CF2_2
   Register : pcie/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_dut/u1_phy/u1_ltssm/u1_osenc/snd_bcn

--------------------------------------------------------------

These components have the GSR property set to DISABLED and are on the inferred
     reset domain. The components will respond to the reset signal 'core_rst_n'
     via the local reset on the component and not the GSR component.
